\section{Full Unconditional Microscopic Closure Theorem}

\section{Statement}

Let the full refined locked TECT linearization be Bloch-Floquet decomposed in the folded Bragg convention
\[
k_*=\frac{G_*}{2},
\qquad
k=k_*+p,
\qquad
|p|\ll |G_*|.
\]
Assume the remote gap condition
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{bench},\rho}^{\mathrm{fin}}>\eta_{R,\rho},
}
\label{eq:U1_gate1}
\end{equation}
so that the low doubled-shell block is spectrally isolated.

Define the exact axial pure-\(JJ\) overlap matrix by
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal M^{(JJ)}_{ab}
:=
\int_{\mathrm{cell}} d^3x\;
e^{-iG_*\cdot x}\,
\overline{u_a^+(x)}\,
\bigl(\hat n^i K_i^{(\mathrm{II},J)}(x)\bigr)\,
u_b^-(x),
\qquad a,b=1,2.
}
\label{eq:U1_MJJ}
\end{equation}
Then
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
m_3
=
-\frac{1}{2\Gamma_J}
\Bigl(
\mathcal M^{(JJ)}_{11}-\mathcal M^{(JJ)}_{22}
\Bigr).
}
\label{eq:U1_m3}
\end{equation}

Define the exact transverse shell-derivative block
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal T_\nu
:=
\left.\partial_{p_\nu}\widehat\Sigma_{JK}(G_*;p)\right|_{p=0}
+
\left.\partial_{p_\nu}\widehat\Sigma_{KK}(G_*;p)\right|_{p=0},
\qquad
\nu=1,2.
}
\label{eq:U1_Tnu}
\end{equation}
Its shell-adapted Pauli projections are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
c_E
=
\frac14\Tr(\sigma_1\mathcal T_1+\sigma_2\mathcal T_2),
\qquad
c_O
=
\frac14\Tr(\sigma_2\mathcal T_1-\sigma_1\mathcal T_2).
}
\label{eq:U1_cEcO}
\end{equation}

Finally let
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal M_D
=
\mathrm{span}_{\mathbb R}
\{\tau_x\otimes\mathbf 1_2,\tau_y\otimes\mathbf 1_2\},
\qquad
A_{\mathrm{res}}
=
\{K\in\mathrm{Herm}(4):U(g)KU(g)^{-1}=K\ \forall g\in G_{\mathrm{res}}\}.
}
\label{eq:U1_massspace}
\end{equation}

Then the full microscopic TECT linearization contains a spectrally isolated protected anisotropic massless Dirac block whenever
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{bench},\rho}^{\mathrm{fin}}>\eta_{R,\rho},
\qquad
\mathcal M^{(JJ)}_{11}\neq \mathcal M^{(JJ)}_{22},
\qquad
(c_E,c_O)\neq(0,0),
\qquad
A_{\mathrm{res}}\cap\mathcal M_D=\{0\}.
}
\label{eq:U1_master}
\end{equation}

\section{Proof}

By \eqref{eq:U1_gate1}, the low doubled-shell block is spectrally isolated from the remote sector,
so the reduced shell carrier statement is legitimate.

The pure-\(JJ\) sector is axial only, and at principal shell order it feeds only the longitudinal singlet;
therefore
\[
m_3\neq 0
\Longrightarrow
\lambda_\parallel\neq 0.
\]
By \eqref{eq:U1_m3}, this is equivalent to
\[
\mathcal M^{(JJ)}_{11}\neq \mathcal M^{(JJ)}_{22}.
\]

The naive local real Hermitian \(JK\) term vanishes by Pauli anticommutation,
so the honest transverse frontier is exactly the derivative-resolved shell audit.
Thus \((c_E,c_O)\neq (0,0)\) is equivalent to
\[
(\alpha,\beta)\neq (0,0).
\]

Finally, \(A_{\mathrm{res}}\cap\mathcal M_D=\{0\}\) excludes constant Dirac masses on the isolated doubled-shell block.
Hence the reduced principal symbol has the form
\[
\mathcal D_1(p)
=
\lambda_\parallel p_\parallel\,\rho_1\otimes\sigma_3
+
\alpha p_1\,\rho_1\otimes\sigma_1
+
\alpha p_2\,\rho_1\otimes\sigma_2
+
\beta(-p_2\,\rho_1\otimes\sigma_1+p_1\,\rho_1\otimes\sigma_2),
\]
with
\[
\lambda_\parallel\neq 0,
\qquad
(\alpha,\beta)\neq(0,0),
\]
and no allowed constant mass.
Therefore the isolated block is a protected anisotropic massless Dirac block.
\qed

\section{Finite Harmonic Formula for the Unconditional Longitudinal Audit}

Expand the periodic Bloch spinors and the axial pure-\(JJ\) transport input as
\[
u_a^+(x)=\sum_{G\in\mathcal S_N} c_{a,G}^{(+)}e^{iG\cdot x},
\qquad
u_b^-(x)=\sum_{G'\in\mathcal S_N} c_{b,G'}^{(-)}e^{iG'\cdot x},
\]
\[
V_\parallel^{(JJ)}(x):=\hat n^iK_i^{(\mathrm{II},J)}(x)
=
\sum_{Q\in\Lambda^*}\widehat V_\parallel^{(JJ)}(Q)e^{iQ\cdot x}.
\]

Then the exact intervalley overlap is the finite convolution
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal M^{(JJ)}_{ab}
=
V_{\mathrm{cell}}
\sum_{G,G'\in\mathcal S_N}
\overline{c_{a,G}^{(+)}}\,
\widehat V_\parallel^{(JJ)}(G_*+G-G')\,
c_{b,G'}^{(-)}.
}
\label{eq:U1_finite_conv}
\end{equation}

Therefore
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
m_3
=
-\frac{V_{\mathrm{cell}}}{2\Gamma_J}
\sum_{G,G'\in\mathcal S_N}
\Bigl(
\overline{c_{1,G}^{(+)}}c_{1,G'}^{(-)}
-
\overline{c_{2,G}^{(+)}}c_{2,G'}^{(-)}
\Bigr)
\widehat V_\parallel^{(JJ)}(G_*+G-G').
}
\label{eq:U1_m3_finite}
\end{equation}

So the unconditional longitudinal frontier is literally one finite harmonic sum.

\section{Finite Unconditional Transverse Audit}

Define
\[
\mathcal T_\nu
=
\left.\partial_{p_\nu}\widehat\Sigma_{JK}(G_*;p)\right|_{0}
+
\left.\partial_{p_\nu}\widehat\Sigma_{KK}(G_*;p)\right|_{0},
\qquad \nu=1,2.
\]

Then the exact transverse witnesses are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
c_E
=
\frac14\Tr(\sigma_1\mathcal T_1+\sigma_2\mathcal T_2),
\qquad
c_O
=
\frac14\Tr(\sigma_2\mathcal T_1-\sigma_1\mathcal T_2).
}
\end{equation}

Hence the unconditional transverse pass condition is exactly
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
(c_E,c_O)\neq(0,0).
}
\end{equation}

Inside the explicit folded-Bragg Class II realization, the derivative bookkeeping compresses to
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\widehat T^\alpha_{(II)}(G_*)
=
-\frac{\alpha_X\beta_X}{M_X^2}
\sum_A\sum_{Q+Q'=G_*}
\widehat J_i^A(Q)\widehat K_{i,\alpha}^A(Q'),
\qquad \alpha=1,2,
}
\end{equation}
so the practical explicit reduction
\[
A_{G_*}(C_1\!\cdot\!G_*)\neq0,
\qquad
A_{G_*}(C_2\!\cdot\!G_*)\neq0
\]
is just the first-shell compressed version of the unconditional derivative audit.

\section{Gate 3: Full Unconditional Transverse Pass Sheet}

\section{1. Honest microscopic frontier}

The uploaded notes explicitly show that the naive undifferentiated local real Hermitian \(JK\) bilinear vanishes:

+

Therefore the transverse witness cannot be certified from an undifferentiated local \(JK\) term.
The honest microscopic frontier is exactly the derivative-resolved shell audit:

\section{2. Exact witness projections}

Pauli-decompose the derivative shell tensors as
\begin{equation}
\mathcal S_\bullet^{(XY)}
=

+

\qquad

The reduced transverse dictionary is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\alpha=c_E I_\theta,
\qquad

\end{equation}

Therefore the exact transport-side transverse pass condition is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
(c_E,c_O)\neq(0,0).

\label{eq:G3_transport_pass}
\end{equation}

Hence the unconditional transverse problem is completely explicit:

\paragraph{Final verdict.}

\end{equation}
